***возразить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возразить.html>возрази́ть</a> (1576)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">воз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разить.html>рази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Originally meant "to strike back".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возразить.html>возрази́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozrazítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возражать.html>возража́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to object, to mind, to protest</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возрасти.html>возрасти́</a> (7093)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">воз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расти.html>расти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возрасти.html>возрасти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozrastí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возрастать.html>возраста́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grow up</li>
<li>to increase, to rise</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возродить.html>возроди́ть</a> (14778)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">воз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">re-, returning</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>роди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rodítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">give birth to</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возродить.html>возроди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozrodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возрождать.html>возрожда́ть</a></b>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возродить.html>возроди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozrodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возыметь.html>возыме́ть</a> (28291)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">воз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">imétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***воин.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:воин.html>во́ин</a> (2076)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">воинъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voinŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vojinъ</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weyh₁-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воин.html>во́ин</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vóin</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воин.html>во́ина</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воин.html>во́ины</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воин.html>во́инов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>soldier, warrior, serviceman, military man</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:боец.html>бое́ц</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bojéc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воитель.html>вои́тель</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">voítelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военнослужащий.html>военнослу́жащий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vojennoslúžaščij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:солдат.html>солда́т</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">soldát</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***войско.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>во́йско</a> (913)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">воиско</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voisko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vojьsko</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vojьskъ</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*voj-</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ьskъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>во́йско</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vójsko</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>во́йска</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>войска́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:войско.html>во́йск</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:войсковой.html>войсково́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> army, host
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:армия.html>а́рмия</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ármija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> troops, forces</li></ol>

***вокзал.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вокзал.html>вокза́л</a> (1760)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Vauxhall</i> (former site of a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vauxhall_Gardens" class="extiw" title="w:Vauxhall Gardens">pleasure garden</a>). The ending was influenced by <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зал.html>зал</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zal</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The spelling <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">фоксал</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">foksal</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> attested in 1777 is from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">facs-hall</i>, from the same English source. The transportation sense derives from an epithet for the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pavlovsk,_Saint_Petersburg" class="extiw" title="w:Pavlovsk, Saint Petersburg">Pavlovsk</a> train station building, which at one time served as both a passenger lounge and a place of entertainment.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вокзал.html>вокза́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vokzál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вокзал.html>вокза́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вокзал.html>вокза́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вокзал.html>вокза́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> park, pleasure garden
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1813</b>,  Aleksandr Pushkin,  <cite>To Natalie</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гулянье.html>гуля́ньях</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иль.html>иль</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b>воксалах</b> / <a href = vnd.unilang:легкое.html>Лёгким</a> зефи́ром <a href = vnd.unilang:летать.html>лета́л</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na guljánʹjax ilʹ v <b>voksalax</b> / Lexkim zefírom letál.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">At fetes and in <b>parks</b>, I've been flitting like a gentle zephyr.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transport</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> station, terminal <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with a building for passenger facilities</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<ol><li>train station, railroad station, railway station, depot <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with a building for passenger facilities</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:станция.html>ста́нция</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stáncija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
